  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f9bf5e61-d309-4c5c-8b80-ee71127f3fc4'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer7271245643222062817">A series of murders in New York City has stymied the police and FBI alike, and they suspect the culprit is a single killer sending an indecipherable message. But when the two federal agents assigned to the investigation are taken out, the FBI takes a more personal interest in the case.<br/><br/>Special Agent Ty Grady is pulled out of undercover work after his case blows up in his fa</span>
  <span id="freeText7271245643222062817" style="display:none">A series of murders in New York City has stymied the police and FBI alike, and they suspect the culprit is a single killer sending an indecipherable message. But when the two federal agents assigned to the investigation are taken out, the FBI takes a more personal interest in the case.<br /><br />Special Agent Ty Grady is pulled out of undercover work after his case blows up in his face. He's cocky, abrasive, and indisputably the best at what he does. But when he's paired with Special Agent Zane Garrett, it's hate at first sight. Garrett is the perfect image of an agent: serious, sober, and focused, which makes their partnership a classic cliche: total opposites, good cop-bad cop, the odd couple. They both know immediately that their partnership will pose more of an obstacle than the lack of evidence left by the murderer.<br /><br />Practically before their special assignment starts, the murderer strikes again this time at them. Now on the run, trying to track down a man who has focused on killing his pursuers, Grady and Garrett will have to figure out how to work together before they become two more notches in the murderer's knife.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7271245643222062817" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">If your question was a sliding scale between "story ends" and "read the whole series," my answer would be in the middle with a slight edge towards "wh<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">If your question was a sliding scale between "story ends" and "read the whole series," my answer would be in the middle with a slight edge towards "whole series" The crime plot wraps up at the end of the book, but the relationship plot stretches through the series. I would say that they don't even fall in actual love until Divide &amp; Conquer (#4). Several of the later books do have cliff-hangers, but not this one. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=read-m-m">read-m-m</a>
          </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4477450284367642992"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388593i/749186.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><b><br/>This book has a false title! <br/><br/>The real one is: <br/><br/><blockquote><u>Read & Become obsessed with Ty and Zane!</u></blockquote>
<br/><br/><br/>I just felt like I should warn anyone who's thinking of reading the book :)</b><br/><br/><br/>Hello, I am a Ty and Zane addict. I have been an addict for 3 days now, and I'm trying not to cure myself. It's not very easy, considering I have only 5 books more to read, and then I'll go through withdrawal. I guess I'll have to do massive re-reads to keep my addiction. It's not something I'll want to get rid of <a href='http://beta.photobucket.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749187.gif' alt=' photo 805735.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>How my addiction h</span>
  <span id="freeText4477450284367642992" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388593i/749186.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b><br>This book has a false title! <br><br>The real one is: <br><br><blockquote><u>Read &amp; Become obsessed with Ty and Zane!</u></blockquote>
<br><br><br>I just felt like I should warn anyone who's thinking of reading the book :)</b><br><br><br>Hello, I am a Ty and Zane addict. I have been an addict for 3 days now, and I'm trying not to cure myself. It's not very easy, considering I have only 5 books more to read, and then I'll go through withdrawal. I guess I'll have to do massive re-reads to keep my addiction. It's not something I'll want to get rid of <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749187.gif" alt=" photo 805735.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>How my addiction happened? Read the story of a journey of one woman, reading about two men falling in love. Try not to cry very much, and fan yourself when it gets too hot. <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749188.gif" alt=" photo fansmiley.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>The story</b><br><br>Ty and Zane are two FBI agents, forced to work together on a serial-killer case. They are complete opposites. Ty is rough, doesn't follow any rules and doesn't care about anything. Zane is a serious guy, trying to save his career and is looking forward to a promotion, instead he got Ty <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380380814ra/737823.gif" alt=" photo 425845.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> The instant they meet sparks fly all over. They have the most amazing chemistry! <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749189.gif" alt=" photo 2783945661.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Even though they spent half of the book bickering and fighting, it was there all the same. While I'm mentioning the fighting - there was a scene when those two actually fought, as in - kicking ass, and WOW even though the scene wasn't actually sexual, they were pretty much beating each other, it was SO HOT <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749190.gif" alt=" photo 72866.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> or maybe I'm just so bad <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749187.gif" alt=" photo 805735.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> Aaaanyway, back to the chemistry, it was building and building and then came the first kiss - BAM! Supernova! <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749191.gif" alt=" photo explosionta5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> I haven't read many M/M sex scenes (yet <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380380814ra/737815.gif" alt=" photo 703126.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>) but that one was HOOOOOT!<br><br><br>I won't go further than that with the story, it'll ruin the surprise when you get to it, but I'll just say that Ty and Zane are some of the best characters I've read. They are complex, with actuall problems and conflictions, dealing with addiction and PTSD, and their attraction <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/529986.gif" alt=" photo 836920.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I just LOVE them <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749189.gif" alt=" photo 2783945661.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Why 4 stars?</b> The story was kinda bad, not that bad but still it got on my nerves sometimes <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a> And the bad guy - I knew it from the beginning who it was, and was he just terrible <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749193.gif" alt=" photo 750195.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388593ra/749193.gif" alt=" photo 750195.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>BUT, I'm continuing with the series (gotta keep my addiction, you understand), so I'm looking forward to better mysteries and plots :) And, of course, more TY and Zane <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_145764113" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/145764113" />
    <a title="Cheryl" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4613199-cheryl"><img alt="Cheryl" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377316906p2/4613199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/145764113?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cheryl" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cheryl" href="/user/show/4613199-cheryl">Cheryl</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/5199023-cut-run">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4613199-cheryl?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer145764113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14584927938302250718">This book came highly recommended, so I was quite disappointed when I finally got around to reading it. This could have been a really good story, instead it was the literary equivalent of a summer blockbuster movie, complete with requisite car chase/slow-motion car flipping over scene. This was basically every buddy cop movie you've ever seen, except this time the two agents have sex. The two agents would have been interesting characters if the dialogue hadn't been designed to beat you over the </span>
  <span id="freeText14584927938302250718" style="display:none">This book came highly recommended, so I was quite disappointed when I finally got around to reading it. This could have been a really good story, instead it was the literary equivalent of a summer blockbuster movie, complete with requisite car chase/slow-motion car flipping over scene. This was basically every buddy cop movie you've ever seen, except this time the two agents have sex. The two agents would have been interesting characters if the dialogue hadn't been designed to beat you over the head with the fact that these two guys don't like each other, no really, they don't like each other, look at how much they don't like each other! It was fine, if a little cliched, at first, but then it just kept going. Every time I started getting into the book, something would pull me out of it. There is a lot of extremely unlikely dialogue. For example, I doubt two guys who really don't like each other( no really, they really don't like each other) and are trying to keep their bisexuality under wraps would spend so much time joking about each other's butts. Also, while talking to younger FBI agents, one of the main characters mentions that while the younger man was watching cartoons, he was "in the Gulf", to which the other agent replies "The gulf of what?" Not a very likely response from anyone, especially an FBI agent. The authors' depiction of New York City doesn't ring true at all. Where in The Village do you pull out of your parking space into 60mph traffic? And why are there so many hippies still hanging around? And apparently, if you grab a stewardess's butt and then call her sweetheart or darling or something else cliche and insulting, she will give you her phone number and invite you to her affordable-on-a-flight-attendant's-salary Manhattan apartment for anonymous sex. Also in this world, if you are an FBI agent you never have to go to the hospital. After your car is smashed an EMT will set your broken arm and send you home with a bottle of painkillers that they carry with them, even after you tell them you have a previous drug problem, because ambulances are also portable pharmacies, and you don't need X-rays of your broken arm or broken ribs or maybe dislocated shoulder or banged up knee or any of the other injuries you've sustained. And then, when all these things hurt really bad and you just can't take it anymore, you can take the whole bottle of painkillers at once, and this will clear your head and enable you to use your broken arm. <br /><br />I generally don't read mysteries, and this book tried really hard to make sure I don't start. Some of the ways the serial killer murdered his victims were just plain ridiculous, and I don't see how no one picked up on the pattern before the main characters did. And how on earth do you dye someone's hair after you've killed them? Are you lugging dead bodies around the apartment, propping them up in the shower or rinsing their hair in the kitchen sink? This is definately not the book to read if you're looking for a good mystery. <br /><br />As other reviewers have mentioned, POV switches constantly, sometimes in the same paragraph. I'm all for knowing what's going on inside people's heads, just not all at once. I felt like the editors should have picked up on that and helped the authors clear it up a bit. Then again, they should have picked up on a few of the other things I've mentioned, as well.<br /><br />Despite all this, I *wanted* to like this book. I really did. Through all the forced machismo, there is some actual character development. If you like blockbusters and cop movies and have a superhuman ability to suspend disbelief, there are a few good spots in this book. It's refreshing when the characters drop the attitudes and act like real people for a few pages. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14584927938302250718" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7990690051576640414"><b>Aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaahhhhhhhhhhhhhhh...........!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>HOLY MOTHER OF JESUS....all my brain cells have just FRIED!!!</b><br/><br/><b>Phew!!Just give me one second......</b><br/><br/>O.k..so where was I???Oh yes...<br/><br/><br/><b>Readers please make way for this AMAZING,SPECTACULAR and DYNAMIC DUO---<br/><br/><u><i>Ty AND Zane</i></u><br/><br/>HOT!!!<br/><br/>ARMED AND DANGEROUS!!!<br/><br/>GORGEOUS!!!<br/><br/><br/>Careful ladies.....don't SWOON!!(But if a pair of strong arms is nearby to catch you then by all means,be my guest)</b><br/><br/><i>Have you ever HATED someone at first sight???</i><br/><br/>Well FBI agents Ty Grady and Zane Garret</span>
  <span id="freeText7990690051576640414" style="display:none"><b>Aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaahhhhhhhhhhhhhhh...........!!!!!!</b><br><br><b>HOLY MOTHER OF JESUS....all my brain cells have just FRIED!!!</b><br><br><b>Phew!!Just give me one second......</b><br><br>O.k..so where was I???Oh yes...<br><br><br><b>Readers please make way for this AMAZING,SPECTACULAR and DYNAMIC DUO---<br><br><u><i>Ty AND Zane</i></u><br><br>HOT!!!<br><br>ARMED AND DANGEROUS!!!<br><br>GORGEOUS!!!<br><br><br>Careful ladies.....don't SWOON!!(But if a pair of strong arms is nearby to catch you then by all means,be my guest)</b><br><br><i>Have you ever HATED someone at first sight???</i><br><br>Well FBI agents Ty Grady and Zane Garret have.<b>Each other.</b>They were partnered to investigate the Tri-State case.A serial killer was loose and FBI suspected that it was someone on the inside.So,these two agents were called forth to investigate the case,both superb in their respective skills,but....both are LOOSE CANNONS!!<br><br>Being an ex-marine and years of undercover work had provided Ty Grady will lethal skills and sharply honed instincts.But after the death of his last partner,he still lives with the guilt and does not want any new partner.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Specially not one with a stick up his ass!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Zane Garret has his own skills with a sharp mind and indomitable will.But after the death of his wife 5 years ago he had lost it.But then somehow he managed to get rid of his addictions and put his life back on track.(Little did he realize that he was only a shadow of the man he used to be.)And after working so hard,he wasn't going to let a rude,irritating partner destroy everything!!<br><br><i>
  <b>"Listen up,cause I'm only gonna say this once,"Ty muttered."I don't talk when I fly.I sleep.And I don't listen when I eat,understand?I don't wanna be buddies.I don't wanna chat."</b>
</i><br><br>Well,this was their start....<br><br>Everyone thought they were destined to kill each other!!<br><br>But this killer is smarter and more resourceful than they thought.So they have to call a temporary truce to thwart him and save their lives!!<br><br>But no one,not even Ty and Zane could anticipate the fierce attraction which blossomed between them......<br><br><b>
  <i>"Fuck,"Zane murmured,pulling Ty closer." You're worse than heroin."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>Hmmm...my heart is still singing!!!</b><br><br><br><b>Tyyyy annnnd Zaneeeeee.......la,la,la!!!</b><br><br><br>Ahm...**cough**.Sorry,I just got a bit carried away!!<br><br>But how can I help it when they say things like--<br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm too stubborn to die when I have a reason to live," he murmured,watching Ty reverently.<br><br>"I need you,Ty,more than anything."</i>
</b><br><br>***sigh***<br><br>And to all my GR friends who recommended this book to me--<br><br>THANK YOU SO MUCH!!<br><br><br><b>---4 STARS + <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397264i/766381.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> (1 more for Ty and Zane!!)---</b><br><br><br>So go,go,go.....and grab this book right now!!!I promise you that it's amazing!!!<br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1054245794110092921"><blockquote><b>Granted, I'm nine years late to the party and my review may be surplus to requirements but, here it is anyway.</b><br/><br/>Despite the burning need to DNF, I hung in there, soldering through the pages of wince-inducing prose but at page 204, I admitted defeat. This book and I agreed to never speak on the matter again.<br/><br/><b>Allow me to <i>show</i> you why (excerpts from page 203-4, emphasis by me):</b><br/><br/><br/>Ty glanced over at it and immediately groaned <u>softly</u><br/>**<br/>Ty frowned <u>doubtfully.</u> He worked <u>quickly</u> and <u>finally</u> pulled the wound to</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1054245794110092921" style="display:none"><blockquote><b>Granted, I'm nine years late to the party and my review may be surplus to requirements but, here it is anyway.</b><br /><br />Despite the burning need to DNF, I hung in there, soldering through the pages of wince-inducing prose but at page 204, I admitted defeat. This book and I agreed to never speak on the matter again.<br /><br /><b>Allow me to <i>show</i> you why (excerpts from page 203-4, emphasis by me):</b><br /><br /><br />Ty glanced over at it and immediately groaned <u>softly</u><br />**<br />Ty frowned <u>doubtfully.</u> He worked <u>quickly</u> and <u>finally</u> pulled the wound together....<br />**<br />Ty <u>simply</u> nodded and went....to retrieve a glass. He filled it from a bottle that sat on the counter and handed it <u>wordlessly</u> to Zane. <br />**<br />Zane lowered the glass and looked at Ty <u>appraisingly.</u> <br />**<br />Depends on what kind of action you’re talking about,” he said, being <u>deliberately</u> vague. <br /> **<br />“Tough guy, huh?” Ty asked <u>sarcastically</u><br /><b><br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br />.<br /><br /><br />Sigh. I have never read a book that had this many adverbs, sometimes a page would have over 10 of such. <br /><br />Here's the thing: I wouldn't have fixated on those pesky words had the plot and characters been developed beyond the pedestrian.</b><br /><br />TY and Zane are FBI agents who were drafted in to find a serial killer. Ty is the usual wisecracking bad-boy agent while Zane was the "suit". <br /><br />Sound familiar? Think Riggs and Murtaugh- of Lethal Weapon- without the charm, wit, and intelligence.<br /><br />Theirs was an enemies-to-lovers story, sadly, once they got together the plot became secondary turning this into nothing more than a B-rated erotica.<br /><br /><b>The story never advanced beyond their sleeping together. Even when the killer attempted to blow them up, there was no urgency. No rallying of agents or gathering of intel, they basically <s>hid</s> stayed at the hotel to read "files". <br /><br />I say this with all due respect but I doubt the author did any research on the subject matter. Altogether, very sloppy. </b></blockquote></span>

<div id="review_227608333" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/227608333" />
    <a title="Adrian Anderson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5178793-adrian-anderson"><img alt="Adrian Anderson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1349731436p2/5178793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/227608333?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Adrian Anderson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Adrian Anderson" href="/user/show/5178793-adrian-anderson">Adrian Anderson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5178793-adrian-anderson?shelf=not-worth-the-time-i-spent-reading">not-worth-the-time-i-spent-reading</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer227608333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5477125521684075817">This book was a major disappointment. Yet again I have learnt not to trust the high star ratings on Goodreads. They just are too skewed in opinion. The ones who like the book rate it up...and most of the people who hate or dislike it don't even bother to waste their time rating it down - hence the misleading ratings.<br/><br/>I'll try to avoid (major) spoilers. I disliked everything about this book, from the crappy cover art to the poor characterization and plot. I know I complain about the male torsos be</span>
  <span id="freeText5477125521684075817" style="display:none">This book was a major disappointment. Yet again I have learnt not to trust the high star ratings on Goodreads. They just are too skewed in opinion. The ones who like the book rate it up...and most of the people who hate or dislike it don't even bother to waste their time rating it down - hence the misleading ratings.<br /><br />I'll try to avoid (major) spoilers. I disliked everything about this book, from the crappy cover art to the poor characterization and plot. I know I complain about the male torsos being HELLA overused. But after seeing that cover - I take it back. Unappealing, plain and unimaginative. <br /><br />The book was so unbelievably stilted and manufactured. It was as if the authors took the readers for gullible, starry eyed idiots. I agree with those below who said the mystery was not "mysterious" - I have seen Scooby Doo episodes that were more enigmatic. The mystery aspect of the book needed some more planning and development if Roux and Urban expected to captivate anyone with a mental age over 12 with it.<br /><br />This book really made me wonder - ARE two head's better than one? I never was a fan of multi-authored books because if the authors don't mesh the work turns out to be crap with a lot of convoluted rigmarole. And don't get me started on the medical aspects of the book - as a medical student it is a sore point for me. Authors are expected to RESEARCH - it is as SIMPLE AS WIKIPEDIA IF YOU HAVE TO.<br /><br />Double fracture, refusing pain meds even then because of your addiction past...despite being told repeatedly local analgesia won't act centrally and tickle the pleasure centers? I don't buy it. That injury would make BABIES of the toughest men. Spend a few months in orthopedics and then tell me different. The believable thing would be to have accepted the local after some badgering - but NO. Roux and Urban had to use it and play it up YET AGAIN to show us - LOOK HOW TOUGH MY BOY IS.<br /><br />This bit irritated me - "He wove dangerously as he headed to the door, the drugs already taking effect since he’d bypassed the time release by chewing them up. By the time he got to the elevator, the high was rushing through him."<br /><br />Yes, that is SURE to make someone more effective on the field. A HIGH rushing through you? From what I understand, the MC is exhusted and in pain, over doses on pills and becomes superman rather than fall into a coma like we mortals would? Unbelievable.<br /><br />Buried under all the pseudo machismo and crudity the characters are dull. I don't get the feeling I really know them. And you need to KNOW characters to like them. The rest of the cast are the same and can only be referred to as a clip on cast in a failed attempt to inject some interest into the book.<br /><br />And the weird mood swings! I mean really! Are these men or a bunch of bipolar patients? FBI agents need to be mentally stable, right?<br /><br />I won't even go into the childish and dumb dialog (much) :| Aren't you glad? But I will mention this - girls, WOMEN COO, BABIES COO, PIGEONS COO, CUCCOO's COO - men 99.9% of times DO NOT COO. One can only hope their writing (they DO seem to write a lot together don't they) improved after this fiasco.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5477125521684075817" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I liked it, A LOT, but didn't love it. I looooooved their love story but the case they were working on was kinda boring for me and I knew, I freaking knew who the bad guy was!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402070i/781256.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Cut &amp; Run tells us the story of Ty &amp; Zane *SIGH*. They have to work together on a new case and they basically don't like each other, period.<br><br><b>Respectfully, sir, I understand you need someone riding hers on this... agent. But what am I supposed to learn from him?"<br><br>"You can learn to kiss my ass. Just like you do everyone else's" </b><br><br>You see? They tease each other ALL the time and I LOVED that part of the book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402070i/781257._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are fighting all the time and boy, it was soooooo funny! Ty is the biggest smart ass ever but I still love Zane the most :)<br><br><b>"I've never made fun of you. Making fun of you would imply that something about you is fun"</b><br><br>And sometimes their teasing was more than fun, it was hawt!<br><br><b>”He suggested putting you out of your misery”<br>“Your gun ain’t big enough, son”<br>“At the risk of sounding clichéd, I’ve never had that complain before”<br>“I’ll believe that when I see it” </b><br><br>Oh, Ty, you’ll see it and you’ll LOVE it as much as I did!<br><br><b>”Usually I don’t bother people I want to see naked” </b><br><br>As days go by their relationship starts to change and even if they still keep the teasing, they also like each other, and their chemistry is SOOOOO GOOD!<br><br>And then, the inevitable happened and their first was OH MY GOD! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402070i/781258.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>”Should I go back to my room tonight or will we be able to work together and fuck each other senseless at the same time?”</b><br><br>I can’t keep talking about their story (or the case) because I don’t want to spoil you guys but I really recommend this book to all my M/M buddies.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/302047.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> </span>

<div id="review_2552816111" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552816111" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2552816111?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2552816111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5116343498622698744"><i>”We can still cut and run,” he whispered.”</i><br/><br/><u>
  <b>THIS. WAS. PERFECT!!!</b>
</u><br/>It was exactly the kind of book I needed and I’m so happy I finally started to read this series! <b>“Cut & Run”</b> had everything I craved for and I can’t believe it took me so long to get to it! <br/><br/>I mean:<br/>- Two MC’s to die for - check<br/>- An m/m relationship - check<br/>- Action and drama - check<br/>- A plot that forced me to guess about the killer’s identity – check<br/>- Unbearable tension and suspenseful moments – check<br/><br/>Gosh, this was just so, so, so d</span>
  <span id="freeText5116343498622698744" style="display:none"><i>”We can still cut and run,” he whispered.”</i><br /><br /><u>
  <b>THIS. WAS. PERFECT!!!</b>
</u><br />It was exactly the kind of book I needed and I’m so happy I finally started to read this series! <b>“Cut &amp; Run”</b> had everything I craved for and I can’t believe it took me so long to get to it! <br /><br />I mean:<br />- Two MC’s to die for - check<br />- An m/m relationship - check<br />- Action and drama - check<br />- A plot that forced me to guess about the killer’s identity – check<br />- Unbearable tension and suspenseful moments – check<br /><br />Gosh, this was just so, so, so damn good! That’s how I like my books!! Fast and action-packed with lots of soft and tender moments and two MC’s that both have a big mouth! *lol* <br /><br />But tell you what? The best part about his book was Ty Grady!! I love Ty, I want his babies, oh boy this man is so swoon-worthy, I can’t even!!! &lt;333<br /><br /><i>”Zane stood there for a moment, mouth slightly agape. Ty Grady was a rude, insufferable, egoistical, stinking son of a bitch, and Zane was going to need to figure out how to tune him out. Otherwise, he just might give in to the pressure and kill the bastard, for the good of humanity.”</i><br /><br />I loved how he didn’t give a damn about anything; how he hid his soft side under thousands of layers no one was able to penetrate. Well, no one except of Zane of course! ;-P (Was that a pun? Sorry, my fault! *lol*) And haha I almost died laughing when he told Zane that he’s a <b>“lethal weapon”</b>, but damn me if this isn’t the truth! That man had so many amazing skills I couldn’t help but be awestruck whenever I discovered another side of him. I guess I know how Zane felt, because I felt exactly the same way. XD<br /><br /><i>”When he was younger, Ty had allowed himself to enjoy the company of both men and women, whichever struck his fancy at the time. But all his time in the Marine Corps had forced him to suppress many of those feelings.”</i><br /><br />And can we appreciate the fact that both, Zane as well as Ty, are bisexual?! <b>YAY!!!</b> Finally two bisexual characters that are falling hard for each other! &lt;3 I think this was awesome. I mean the word is never mentioned but we know that Zane had a wife and we can see that Ty is more than just inclined towards both sexes as well. ;-) Oh, and their chemistry!!! Boy, how those two had me in tears at some points of the story. It wasn’t all just carnal action, no, those two had deep feelings for each other and it showed! <br /><br /><i>”Shut up,” Ty hissed in response as his entire body turned over into tackle mode and drove all other thoughts from his mind. He ducked his head to lick a trail of water running down Zane’s collarbone and then bit him lightly.”</i><br /><br /><i>”I can’t concentrate on anything, not when all I can think about is you.”</i><br /><br /><i>”Zane swallowed hard as he slid his hand to take Ty’s and lace their fingers together. “Are you feeling this too?” he asked, echoing what they’d asked each other months ago, only to have it pushed aside. But not forgotten.”</i><br /><br />I cried so much when I read this scene. I swear sometimes while reading this I was certain that Zane and Ty would be the death of me. Especially the moment when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ty refused to leave Zane in the car and wrapped his body around him in order to protect him from the impact of the killer’s taxi. And oh my, when Zane called him baby for the first time… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Hell, they are everything!! Those two boys stole my heart and I can’t wait to read the rest of this series, especially because their easy banter is so awesome as well. *lol*<br /><br /><i>”Yeah, well, if you weren’t such a dick…,” Ty murmured with a small smile.<br />Zane snickered. “Works out well since you’re an asshole.”<br />“We’re gonna have to talk about these puns.” Ty groaned as he pulled away and shuffled slowly for the bed.</i><br /><br /><i>”You were a Recon in the Marines and undercover for the FBI, and you’ve never had a concussion? How the hell did you manage that?”<br />“I ducked,” Ty answered in a childishly honest voice.<br />“You ducked,” Zane muttered. “Smartass.”</i><br /><br />I swear I laughed so much whenever they exchanged their pleasantries that my hubby gave me funny looks while I read the book. *lol* But I also cried while reading it so yeah, I bet he must have been very confused watching my reactions. Haha! Also, I <u>KNEW</u> who the killer was!!! YAY me! I’m getting good at this guessing and puzzle game. Guess that’s what too many CSI, Castle and Sherlock Holmes episodes will do to you. XD<br /><br />All told, I loved this book to bits and pieces and I didn’t want it to end! Thankfully it seems like there are 8 other books still waiting to be read! YESH!!! *does a happy dance* I’m so going to savour them all! This was just the beginning! ;-)<br />____________________________<br /><br /><b>PRE-REVIEW:</b><br /><br />I have this sudden urge to read another m/m romance.<br />It's been a while and I feel like I just need the gay! <br /><br />And because I would trust <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66216992-wynne-katherine" rel="nofollow noopener">THIS AWESOME GIRL</a> with my <s>gay</s> life when it comes to amazing m/m books I decided to give this a shot!<br />Finally! <br /><br />I'm sure you already waited for me to read this, am I right? *lol*</span>
  <a data-text-id="5116343498622698744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_359231484" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/359231484" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4878104-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515345527p2/4878104.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/359231484?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/4878104-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=dude-where-is-the-plot">dude-where-is-the-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=mc-with-an-average-iq-of-80">mc-with-an-average-iq-of-80</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=shouldve-donated-to-wwf-instead">shouldve-donated-to-wwf-instead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=gotta-get-through-this">gotta-get-through-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=first-time-gay">first-time-gay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=juvenile-adults">juvenile-adults</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=everyone-liked-it-but-me">everyone-liked-it-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=whine-like-its-1999">whine-like-its-1999</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=pulpy-fun">pulpy-fun</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4878104-kat?shelf=crime-thriller-horror">crime-thriller-horror</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer359231484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer228213817601450887">I do hope Ty carries a chap-stick around at all times, because the guy licked his lips 23 times before I lost count. <br/><br/>Although I got so little enjoyment out of a book that I had anticipated so greatly, I'm still leaning towards giving <i>Cut & Run</i> 2 generous stars. Mostly out of respect for my friends on here who all seem to genuinely like it. And because, I might as well admit it, I feel the need to be a little more supportive towards m/m than f/m romances. <br/><br/>Now that that's settled, let's move on to</span>
  <span id="freeText228213817601450887" style="display:none">I do hope Ty carries a chap-stick around at all times, because the guy licked his lips 23 times before I lost count. <br /><br />Although I got so little enjoyment out of a book that I had anticipated so greatly, I'm still leaning towards giving <i>Cut &amp; Run</i> 2 generous stars. Mostly out of respect for my friends on here who all seem to genuinely like it. And because, I might as well admit it, I feel the need to be a little more supportive towards m/m than f/m romances. <br /><br />Now that that's settled, let's move on to a few of <i>Cut &amp; Run</i>s weaknesses. The writing for example. Apart from Ty licking his lips nervously almost non-stop, he and his partner Zane hardly ever just <i>say</i> something. Instead they murmur, mutter softly, drawl or growl. <br />The POV too, switches so many times - in the same paragraph too - that it's dizzying. As soon as Ty <i>growls</i> something at Zane, the authors want to make sure that it's perfectly obvious how Zane feels about that, by switching to his thoughts and then back again. They also quite suddenly - and unnecessarily - switch to the mind of another cop, that of the serial killer and his victims. Constant POV switches: they so often seem a telltale sign of a not very talented author.<br /><br />Right, the serial killer. The plot revolves around the stereotypical cops Ty and Zane, who are partnered up to catch this culprit. Since they intensely hate each other at first sight (mostly because one of them looks pretty decent and the other all scruffy) working on their new case is a little complicated. It doesn't really matter that much though, because the whole case obviously only serves as a vessel to throw these guys together. They pretend to think about the killers' motives, while hanging around in diners and their hotel room, living on a diet of pizza's and burgers (good luck sustaining those body builder bods, boys!). <br />In the meantime our serial killer randomly kills off victims by - for example - injecting them with the bird flu (he probably bought a potent virus at his local pharmacy?), he has fun dyeing his victims' hair postmortem and he randomly places bombs in computers and cars to destroy our dream-team. Both Zane and Ty get seriously wounded by these attempts, but apparently they are such tough cops that they can cope with just a bottle of painkillers. Clearly, the authors never did any medical research or just didn't care.<br /><br />Sooooo.. there's always still the sex you say? <br /><br />Uhm...well..at some point I read: <i>"Zane tried to decide why this hurt so much. They had known each other barely a week. Granted they had screwed each other like crazy."</i> WAIT <i>fucking</i> WHAT?! Yes, it's true that their instant hate didn't last long at all...but I meant the screwing part. That part Ty later refers to as the <i>"wild fucking"</i> part. Hey, I'm guilty of skimming pages, but surely I didn't miss a couple of steaming sex scenes? <br />Then I figured it's probably a matter of definition. Their definition of hot sex is getting all worked up and then, at the point of no return, one of them asks himself whether <i>"it's a good idea to screw his partner"</i>, or they realize that they are actually very tired, or very wounded (I hardly remember them not being wounded, so go figure), or hungry for more pizza's and burgers, or they find something to argue about and get angry with each other (which unfortunately doesn't result in a dangerously intense hate fuck/make up sex scene either). And when these boys FINALLY managed to ACTUALLY have sex, it was so bland that it barely registered with me. <br /><br />Ty was probably on the same wavelength though, because while attempting to fuck Zane, he simply picked up his buzzing phone (for which alone he deserves to be punched in his heart-shaped face) and talked and listened to a flirt who felt neglected. Crazy sex indeed. But in a different way than I had imagined. <br /><br />Did I mention that <i>Cut &amp; Run</i> is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/145764113" rel="nofollow noopener">chock-full</a> of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/227608333" rel="nofollow noopener">inconsistencies</a>?<br /><br />Forgive me <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/962319.Manna_Francis" rel="nofollow noopener">Manna Francis</a>, I promise I will stray no more until I have finished your mind-blowing series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="228213817601450887" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1721695195" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1721695195" />
    <a title="James" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7365405-james"><img alt="James" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522094190p2/7365405.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1721695195?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="James" class="user" itemprop="url" name="James" href="/user/show/7365405-james">James</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=1-fiction">1-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=3-multi-book-series">3-multi-book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7365405-james?shelf=2-fic-other">2-fic-other</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1721695195" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2660861904615034111"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199022.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_' title='Cut & Run (Cut & Run, #1) by Madeleine Urban' rel='nofollow noopener'>Cut & Run</a> was my second adventure into this type of novel and it kept my interest. The pairing of Ty and Zane are certainly comical but I have to question why there is always so much anger between the two main characters just like in the first novel I read ([book:Shattered Glass|13420351)? I get that it makes good drama for an intense read, but I thought it was a little too overdone. Ty and Zane get together and separate 4 or 5 times in the course of the 350 page novel and by the last one, I fel</span>
  <span id="freeText2660861904615034111" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5199022.Cut___Run__Cut___Run___1_" title="Cut &amp; Run (Cut &amp; Run, #1) by Madeleine Urban" rel="nofollow noopener">Cut &amp; Run</a> was my second adventure into this type of novel and it kept my interest. The pairing of Ty and Zane are certainly comical but I have to question why there is always so much anger between the two main characters just like in the first novel I read ([book:Shattered Glass|13420351)? I get that it makes good drama for an intense read, but I thought it was a little too overdone. Ty and Zane get together and separate 4 or 5 times in the course of the 350 page novel and by the last one, I felt like it was just getting to be a routine with them (and not in a totally good way). Fighting is a good thing in a book as it helps the reader develop passion and intrigue, but not when on full repetition.<br /> <br />Despite those initial thoughts, the dialogue is fairly realistic, the characters have many good qualities and the story was strong. It's easy to guess who the serial murderer is, but I don't think that was the most important part of the book. I'll give the author another read but probably not for a bit while I explore this genre for awhile to find the authors I like the most.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>
    <u>About Me</u>
  </i>
</b><br />For those new to me or my reviews... here's the scoop: I read A LOT. I write A LOT. And now I blog A LOT. And you can find all my social media profiles to get the details on the who/what/when/where and my pictures. Leave a comment and let me know what you think. Vote in the poll and ratings. Thanks for stopping by. <i>Note</i>: All written content is my original creation and copyrighted to me, but the graphics and images were linked from other sites and belong to them. Many thanks to their original creators.</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_212021577" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/212021577" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/212021577?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/5199023-cut-run">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved">books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer212021577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5722441601595184281">"But let there be spaces in your togetherness and let the winds of the heavens dance between you. Love one another but make not a bond of love: let it rather be a moving sea between the shores of your souls."<br/>- by Khalil Gibran, Love Letters in the Sand: The Love Poems of<br/>Khalil Gibran -<br/><br/>FBI Special Agent Tyler Grady is assigned to the Criminal Investigations Branch. FBI Special Agent Zane Garrett is glad to quit his boring-ass desk job at cyber crimes. He’s transferred (promoted) to the Criminal I</span>
  <span id="freeText5722441601595184281" style="display:none">"But let there be spaces in your togetherness and let the winds of the heavens dance between you. Love one another but make not a bond of love: let it rather be a moving sea between the shores of your souls."<br />- by Khalil Gibran, Love Letters in the Sand: The Love Poems of<br />Khalil Gibran -<br /><br />FBI Special Agent Tyler Grady is assigned to the Criminal Investigations Branch. FBI Special Agent Zane Garrett is glad to quit his boring-ass desk job at cyber crimes. He’s transferred (promoted) to the Criminal Investigations Branch and meets...Ty, his new partner.<br /><br />When the two men meet for the first time, they’re shocked to discover that they are 'forced' to work together. Assistant Director Burns is putting them on the Tri-State case. A really messy, conniving, and frightening serial killer is on the loose. The villain is killing people in New York every few weeks. The latest victims are two FBI agents working this case and that means that the Bureau was now more personally invested. Ty and Zane have to replace those two agents who got killed.<br /><br />Ty and Zane are complete opposites. Zane became an alcoholic and did drugs after his wife was killed a few years ago. He doesn’t drink anymore, however he’s a heavy smoker. Zane works by the book, and he works with complete and utter focus; Zane is logical and single-minded. And he is well groomed. Ty is a former Marine Force Recon. He is cocky and a smart-mouth. And he is fun! Ty was bisexual in his youth. He stopped having sex with men after he joined the Marines. Now he’s a bit confused because he’s not all that sure what he really wants: women or men. Zane is only seeing men after his wife's death. Soon after Ty and Zane start working together, they feel attracted to each other. They fight and insult each other but become lovers eventually.<br /><br />An advice to the readers: don’t read this book for the plot, read it for the characters. They are superb – loved them! Ty and Zane were shining! The plot is clearly not as strong as the main characters.<br /><br />I love it when two very tough guys go all tender over each other. Don’t strangle me now when I say that this was sweet. The author writes with great care for tenderness and that’s something I love to read about. Tenderness is...a specific look, a touch, a word. I was very fond of Ty and Zane and I was particularly invested in them. There’s lots and lots of dialogs. Smooth, good, cool, and hilarious dialogs! Yes, there’s a serial killer on the loose but I didn’t really care about that fact. I was captivated by those two guys and their character and 'relationship' development. My oh my, this was a rocky, unsteady, and volatile 'relationship' – laden with a lot of conflicts. They separate and come together. Again. Their relationship is like a moving sea, and therefore I think that the quote I’ve chosen fits rather nicely.<br /><br />They have a lot of interaction and it helps the reader to get to know them. Furthermore, it was rather interesting to see that Ty had to undergo quite a transformation. In the beginning he is this daredevil who doesn’t give a damn about rules. After a specific incident (I can’t give away more here) he is quite the opposite – more detached, as it is. It’s like they switched roles because Zane is more agitated – he’s lacking his usual aloofness. I was wondering if their 'unusual' behavior is only temporary? Maybe this will change again in the sequel.<br /><br />During the second half of the book the dialogs get more serious. The banter is still present but you can feel that there’s just more. A lot of stuff seems to be buried and you’re waiting that everything will have to surface somehow. I’m rather sure that we will unravel a few 'secrets' in book 2, 3, and 4. I don’t want to sound clichéd but this book – specifically the characters, their demeanor, their way to act and speak – is exactly what I would assimilate to a female author in the m-m genre. There are emotions and tenderness and passionate sexd. Women love to chat – generally speaking. There are so many dialogs here, absolutely incredible. But I love that. You feel connected and you are right there with Ty and Zane. This is what makes you believe that you could crawl into their heads and it gives you a feeling what it could mean to live their lives. There is not a lot of sex in this book but I didn’t mind. Not at all. However, what’s there...is really substantial, it is passionate and hot and it’s well written. It is there because it needs to be there. Jeez, I’m a sucker for touching, good hands, good kisses – it’s all there and then some.<br /><br />From the get-go I was absolutely hooked. For the record, I am a Ty person. Ty reminds me a bit of Dan of Special Forces. And Dan is closer to my heart as is Ty now. LOVED their banter – so hilarious!! I think that the character development was good – two very, very MACHO men! <br /><br />Memorable "quotes":<br /><br />[...]"Fortunately for you, Grady you have more lives than a cat,” the man said to him with a small frown. “And you’re getting another chance to prove to us that you can do this job without blowing shit up. I won’t say one more, because God knows I’ll just keep giving you more until you get yourself killed. Meet your new partner, Special Agent Zane Z. Garrett.”<br />Zane couldn’t have been more appalled, and it showed clearly in his reaction. This WRECK of an agent was his new partner? “Director Burns,” he started impulsively, but he caught his tongue and tightened his grip on the chair. What kind of reward was this?<br />“The hell he is!” Ty interrupted as he sat up straight. “I can’t do my job with a...a...poster-boy partner,” he practically stuttered angrily as he flopped his hand toward the squeaky-clean man next to him."[...]<br /><br />[...]"Frankly, it will take a miracle to make him even remotely professional. No one will take him seriously.”<br />“Take ME seriously?” Ty echoed in disbelief. “Christ, have those shoes ever even seen pavement? Shit,” he exclaimed in a sudden panic as he gripped the arms of his chair and leaned forward. “Are you sending me to Cyber?” he asked Burns, who was sitting behind the desk and grinning like a small child at Christmas.[...]<br /><br />[...]”Listen up, ‘cause I’m only gonna say this once,” Ty muttered as they walked to their gate. “I don’t talk when I fly. I sleep. And I don’t listen when I eat, understand? I don’t wanna be buddies, I don’t wanna chat,” he said with a sarcastic lilt to the word. “I don’t wanna know about your childhood or how your momma whipped you with a rubber glove or how much therapy you had to go through ‘cause you flunked out of preschool. I don’t wanna hear about how you want to be Director someday or how many collars you got chasin’ those Internet freaks or how proud you are of your bowel movements. I don’t wanna go shopping at Barney’s with you, and I’m not gonna help you pick out your ties to match your socks and, I swear to God, if you get me shot, I’ll kill you.”[...]<br /><br />[...]”You have absolutely no people skills,” Zane muttered, shaking his head. “No wonder you’re sinking fast in the Bureau.”<br />“Yeah, I’m a real anchor,” Ty drawled as he leaned his head back and smiled. “I hear no one else will work with you.”<br />Zane’s lips pressed together slightly and he didn’t look up from his paperwork. “You should have your hearing checked,” he said flatly.<br />“My hearing’s just fine, Skippy. You were 'promoted', right?” Ty asked sarcastically, giving the word quotations with his fingers without opening his eyes. “Hate to tell you, Sport, but being transferred to another division in the same level ain’t a promotion. It’s called shuffling the unwanted.”<br />“Reliable information, I’m sure, from someone on a landslide down the ladder.”<br />“We both seem to be on the slip 'n' slide to the gutter, Shuffleboard,” Ty observed happily. “Difference is, I don’t give a shit,” [...]<br /><br />[...]”How many harsh words will it take to send you into a bottle?” Ty asked as he yanked his forearm away and smacked at Zane’s hand. “Not too damn many, I’m guessing.”<br />“How many times am I gonna have to rip down those walls you keep putting up before you fucking pop and go ballistic at precisely the wrong time?” Zane snapped, fingers grasping and tightening despite the smack. “How long can you keep it all inside? 'Cause believe me, you’ve got no chance of doing it forever.”<br />Ty reached for Zane’s hand suddenly, squeezing his wrist to free his other hand. As soon as Zane’s fingers let go, Ty reached out and backhanded him.<br />If Zane had been a smaller man, he might have fallen sideways under the blow. As it was, his chin snapped to the side from the strength of it, and when he looked back at Ty, he had to lick a trickle of blood off his split lip. When he spoke, his voice was strong and even with the surety of hard-won personal experience. “If you can’t learn to let go of the anger and frustration somehow, it will eat you up inside,” he adevised. “And I don’t mean hiding in the bottom of a bottle or between some stranger’s thighs.”<br />Ty closed his eyes and looked away, visibly trying to calm himself. “I’m sorry,” he finally murmured. He turned slightly and reached back to Zane, sliding his hand against the side of his face as he wiped the blood away from Zane’s lip with his thumb regretfully.<br />Zane pressed his cheek into Ty’s hand, looking over him with softer eyes, and his mouth quirked. “Well, I deserved it,” he said. “I don’t want you to go through what I did.”[...]<br /><br />[...]”Come here,” he requested, reaching out an arm.<br />Ty glanced over at him to see if he was making light. When he didn’t see any signs of joking he narrowed his eyes slightly. “Fuck off. Priss,” he offered with a small smile.<br />Zane’s eyes sparkled and he laid his hand over his propped-up knee. “Who are you callin' Priss, Mr. Suited Up and Shiny?” he taunted.<br />“If this is going to resort to name-calling, I’ve already got you beat, Spanky,” Ty warned with a smirk.<br />“How do you figure that, Jarhead?” Zane replied.<br />“'Cause I rock,” Ty explained in an even voice. “And you don’t,” he continued as he pointed at Zane, pinky finger held out to the side daintily as if he were drinking tea.<br />Smirking, Zane sat up, grabbed Ty and dragged him down onto the bed and under his bigger body. “I’d poke you, but you’d beat the shit out of me.”<br />Ty flailed briefly before he was pinned, and he blinked up at Zane suspiciously as he flexed his fingers under Zane’s grip. “Power trip,” he accused softly.<br />Zane waggled his eyebrows. “I gave you a chance to come peacefully.”[...]<br /><br /><br />Honestly, Cut &amp; Run is what makes me enjoy the m-m genre. It is not quite on the same level as Zero at The Bone, but to be fair it is a different book. You cannot really compare those two books. Both of them are special in one’s own way. I can’t Cut &amp; Run, either. I must read the sequel "Sticks &amp; Stones"!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5722441601595184281" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3609017431" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11238667752543871130">I am confused. I loved the story itself but the ending felt rushed to me. I loved how creative the author was with the 'Poe' murders and the identity of the killer was something I definitely didn't see coming! This book honestly reminded me how much I love a good murder and I'm so glad I picked it up!<br/><br/>BUT<br/><br/>I did not like the push and pull between them. I felt that Ty was too conflicted with his feelings towards Zane and refused to open up. What I hated most in the book was that both the times they </span>
  <span id="freeText11238667752543871130" style="display:none">I am confused. I loved the story itself but the ending felt rushed to me. I loved how creative the author was with the 'Poe' murders and the identity of the killer was something I definitely didn't see coming! This book honestly reminded me how much I love a good murder and I'm so glad I picked it up!<br /><br />BUT<br /><br />I did not like the push and pull between them. I felt that Ty was too conflicted with his feelings towards Zane and refused to open up. What I hated most in the book was that both the times they were apart, Ty slept with different girls. Added to the fact that he always looked over his shoulder whenever they were in public and never Zane kissed in public. But then again, Ty wasn't the only one to blame in that matter. Like I really wanted them to come out to the world instead of pretending to be people they weren't and be together as a couple instead of just being two people in uncharted territory especially after reading 400 pages. I mean, in the end, they still weren't together and their "relationship" wasn't defined, and I hated that. <br /><br />That being said, overall I enjoyed the book. I wasn't bored for a moment and the book always kept me on my toes, especially with the murders! The characters were definitely loveable, only I felt that some thing's were missing and the ending was rushed. <br /><br />So like I said, <b>3.5 'very confusing' stars.</b><br /><br /><i>P.S: I can't believe that there are 9 books in the series, all following Ty and Zane's story</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16944381022660252293"><b>4,25 stars<br/><br/>I loved it so much! More than I expected actually.</b><br/><br/>I've heard this first book isn't the best in the series and some friends did mention I need to read more to fall completely in love with Ty and Zane.<br/><br/>I had it in my TBR for a very long time. Every time I stumbled upon any of the books in this series from my friends' reviews I wanted to start it right away, BUT for reasons I always postponed. Now I'm sorry I did, because I get why everyone fell for Ty and Zane. <br/><br/>The beginning was too slow.</span>
  <span id="freeText16944381022660252293" style="display:none"><b>4,25 stars<br /><br />I loved it so much! More than I expected actually.</b><br /><br />I've heard this first book isn't the best in the series and some friends did mention I need to read more to fall completely in love with Ty and Zane.<br /><br />I had it in my TBR for a very long time. Every time I stumbled upon any of the books in this series from my friends' reviews I wanted to start it right away, BUT for reasons I always postponed. Now I'm sorry I did, because I get why everyone fell for Ty and Zane. <br /><br />The beginning was too slow. I didn't get into the story quite from the start. First we meet Ty and Zane. They seem so different and bump heads all the time. But I really enjoyed the banter. Ty was super rude. Zane seemed more reserved and tried to control his anger better. At least at first. <br /><br />At about 30% the action started to speed up. I was curious about the serial killer but in the same time I wanted more between them! I was looking forward to their first kiss and I wondered if they'll be just as explosive together. And they were. This book isn't as focused on the romance as I expected. And the sex scenes were only a few, but they were extremely HOT! <br /><br />I'm glad we get many surprises on the way. Unfortunately the killer's identity wasn't one of them. <br />I didn't expect the push and pull between the characters and the dynamic to change so abrupt and for many times. I can't say I was happy with them being apart for months either, but the ending did give me hope they'll <b>
  <i>cut and run</i>
</b> at one point. I so want them together and in love!<br /><br /><b>I'm looking forward to reading more and I really hope we'll get more hot scenes with the two of them in the next books.</b></span>

<div id="review_363227858" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/363227858" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/363227858?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ~ Becs ~ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6875778-monique">Monique</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=scarred-heroes">scarred-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=feebs">feebs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=serial-killer">serial-killer</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=glbt">glbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=biker-hero">biker-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer363227858" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10299210266724116293">I’d heard so much about Zane and Ty in my Goodreads Update Feeds over the last few months, these guys have become almost like rockstars to me. My insatiable curiosity was always going to get the better of me and so I just had to give in and find out for myself what the fuss is all about. Before I even started reading this, the synopsis made me think of the Winchester Brothers and who can resist a bit of Wincest? Zane, at least for me, is Sam and Ty, the wisecracking Dean. With this visual in min</span>
  <span id="freeText10299210266724116293" style="display:none">I’d heard so much about Zane and Ty in my Goodreads Update Feeds over the last few months, these guys have become almost like rockstars to me. My insatiable curiosity was always going to get the better of me and so I just had to give in and find out for myself what the fuss is all about. Before I even started reading this, the synopsis made me think of the Winchester Brothers and who can resist a bit of Wincest? Zane, at least for me, is Sam and Ty, the wisecracking Dean. With this visual in mind, their characters came instantly to life off the page right from the first few paragraphs. I loved them both straight away – it’s hard not to.<br><br>They’re FBI agents thrown together to work a serial killer case as partners. They develop an instant dislike for one another when they first meet. Zane appears neat, well presented, calm, polite, by the book <s>hot</s>, Ty is dishevelled, brash, cocky, <s>hot</s> and a maverick. They appear to be polar opposites but as we get to know them, we realise that they’re not so very different.<br><br>As the days go by, they snipe and bicker continuously at one another – their banter was hilarious, not at all clichéd and I laughed out loud at them so many times. It’s a slow burner but their sexual chemistry builds gradually to an intense crescendo and completely reaches fever pitch to the point that when they finally succumb and Zane tilts his head sideways and slides his lips firmly over Ty’s, I swear I had fireworks and the hallelujah chorus going off in my head. I loved their first sex scene together. You could sense their reluctance to admit what was passing between them but sizzling animal attraction was totally getting the better of them and neither of them can resist and it is so FREAKIN hot!!<br><br>I’ve read reviews for this book where readers have complained that the actual serial killer storyline isn’t strong enough. I have to say that I disagree and thought it was really tense but, while I enjoyed that aspect of the book, this was for me totally 100% about Zane and Ty. The way they prowled around each other trying to ignore their mutual attraction like caged tigers eventually giving into it and the ferocious sex they share almost short-circuited my brain. This is the hottest m-m I have ever read – not just because of the sex, although that is great, but because I loved their characters so much, felt everything that they felt and longed for them to be together. There’s real emotional intensity here. I really felt like I knew them intimately, felt like I was there with them and kind of wished I was. <s> I could be the filling to a Zane and Ty sandwich</s> – scratch that!! Behave Rebecca!<br><br>Even though they’re both incredibly masculine, there’s something really quite tender going on here besides the down and dirty sex scenes – it really touched my heart in a way that no other m-m has yet to date. They both get injured in the line of duty and each takes it in turn to gently tend the other’s wounds. Eventually these injuries get them hauled off the case and sent their separate ways – parting is such sweet sorrow. BUT, it’s an amazing voyage of discovery for them both, a journey well taken, finding each other after loss, pain, addiction and sorrow and allowing themselves to admit the pleasure of each other’s bodies and souls. You can tell how deep their feelings run even when neither of them can say it out loud.<br><br>All the time I was reading it, I just couldn’t get a certain song out of my head. Something about Zane and Ty completely conjured these lyrics for me<br><br><i>Carry on my wayward son<br>There'll be peace when you are done<br>Lay your weary head to rest<br>Don't you cry no more</i><br><br>God, I loved this – I ate up every word. The writers have an incredibly fluid style which picks you up, drags you along and doesn’t let go until the very last word. It’s highly intoxicating and addictive with a central duo that I feel sure will go the distance. I am pretty late arriving at this party and, as such, there are 5 more books and a novella just ‘one click’ away. Happy Days!<br><br>5 star m-m romance of the highest order<br><br>Thanks should go to the lovely Monique who has been trying to get me to read these books for months. You were right sweety x<br><br><br><i> note to self – Zane and Ty not Zy and Tane!</i><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380383156i/741277.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10299210266724116293" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
